[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Java-based fuzzing run triggered an OutOfMemoryError while processing a PDF file [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining a PFB [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrinter Font Binary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m font. The error surfaced in Apache [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap exhaustion.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue: During a fuzzing session managed by Jazzer, the target application ran out[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof Java heap space [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when parsing a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPFB font stream. The fuzzer reported a low-severity security issue labeled “Out of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory [0m[1;39m([0m[39muse ‘-Xmx1710m’ to reproduce[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m”.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type: Resource exhaustion through unbounded memory allocation, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting in a Denial-of-Service condition.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating excessive memory use while interpreting PFB font data.  [0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb = [0m[1;35min.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The root cause of the OutOfMemoryError is the unbounded `[0m[1;35mreadAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min both `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructors. Although [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` enforces a `MAX_LENGTH` check on cumulative segment sizes, the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial read already allocates the entire input into memory, bypassing that guard.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We will introduce a pre‐read size limit—using the same `MAX_LENGTH` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant—to cap upfront allocation. All other parsing logic remains unchanged.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Consolidate constructors[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change the `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructor to delegate to the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`InputStream` constructor rather than calling `Files.readAllBytes`. This ensures [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboth paths share the same size‐limited read logic.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Replace:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          with:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • This applies `MAX_LENGTH` enforcement uniformly for file‐ and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream‐based inputs.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Implement a size‐limited read method[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Introduce a private helper in `PfbParser`:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m[1;35mreadAllBytesWithLimit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in, long maxBytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrows IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new [0m[1;35mByteArrayOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m buffer = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8192[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            long totalRead = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            int n;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mn = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                totalRead += n;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotalRead > maxBytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB data exceeds maximum allowed length:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"[0m[39m + totalRead[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mbaos.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return [0m[1;35mbaos.toByteArray[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use this helper in the `InputStream` constructor:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Replace:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb = [0m[1;35min.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpfb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          with:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              long maxInputSize = MAX_LENGTH + PFB_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_LENGTH;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb = [0m[1;35mreadAllBytesWithLimit[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, maxInputSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpfb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This ensures we never allocate more than `MAX_LENGTH + header` bytes.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Add an extra defense in `parsePfb`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - At the very start of `[0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, add:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpfb.length > MAX_LENGTH + PFB_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB data too large: "[0m[39m + pfb.length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - While largely redundant after the constructor cap, it defends against [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture changes that might bypass the constructor logic.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All downstream parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39msegment‐type checks, per‐segment size bounds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical, preserving PDFBox’s Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font support.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to harness or fuzzing logic; only internal FontBox code is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing unit tests continue to work for fonts under the `MAX_LENGTH` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthreshold.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Side‐Effect Mitigation[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By bounding the upfront read, we prevent heap exhaustion from large or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious PFB streams, directly addressing the OutOfMemoryError.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The chosen buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m KB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m balances I/O efficiency and granularity of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize check.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rejecting inputs larger than `MAX_LENGTH` aligns with the existing [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment‐size policy and fails fast for overly large fonts.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side effect: legitimate PFB fonts slightly above the threshold will [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow be rejected. To mitigate, developers can adjust `MAX_LENGTH` if truly [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnecessary.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. References to Code Ranges[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Constructors in `fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.java` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m93[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m107[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m103[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m110[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `parsePfb` method start [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m124[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - New helper and constructor changes should be added within the same file.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo external libraries or harness code are modified. This targeted patch enforces a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle, unified memory guard and eliminates the root cause of unbounded allocation.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Refactor `PfbParser` to true streaming parsing:**  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Remove the two‐stage buffering** [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitial full read into `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb` + [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper‐segment `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m buf` lists + final `pfbdata` copy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. These triple the memory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfootprint and cause OOME even under the MAX_LENGTH bound.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a single streaming parse method that reads from the `InputStream` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecord by record and writes directly into the final buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor output stream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiscarding each small read buffer as soon as it’s written.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Implementation sketch:**  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Add a new private method, e.g.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private void [0m[1;35mparsePfbStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          long total = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Pre-allocate final buffer or use ByteArrayOutputStream with initial [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcap = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mMAX_LENGTH[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ByteArrayOutputStream out = new [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mByteArrayOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mMath.min[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMAX_LENGTH, Integer.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m buf = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8192[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              int marker = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarker == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarker != START_MARKER[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Start marker [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mmissing"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              int recordType = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecordType == EOF_MARKER[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecordType != ASCII_MARKER && recordType != BINARY_MARKER[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Incorrect record type: "[0m[39m + recordType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m‐byte size little‐endian[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              long size = [0m[1;35mreadUint32LE[0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              long newTotal = total + size;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnewTotal > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB data exceeds maximum allowed length"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m stream the segment:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecordType == BINARY_MARKER[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m raw copy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35mcopyFully[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, out, size, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ASCII: perform clear‐to‐mark conversion inline[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35mclearToMarkStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, out, size, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              total = newTotal;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          pfbdata = [0m[1;35mout.toByteArray[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. **Helper methods:**  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mreadUint32LE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` reads four bytes and constructs a `long`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mcopyFully[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, out, size, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` loops `[0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39msize>[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, reads `n = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mmin[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf.length, size[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, `[0m[1;35mout.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf,[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, `size -= n`.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mclearToMarkStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, out, size, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` replicates existing [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mclearToMark[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` logic but processes in‐stream: read chunks, scan for [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend‐of‐ASCII marker, filter CR/LF, write to `out`, and discard.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Wire the streaming parser:**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructors, *remove* any eager `readAllBytes` or `readAllBytesWithLimit` calls. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInstead, directly call `[0m[1;35mparsePfbStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Drop** the old `[0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method or leave it deprecated for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackward compatibility [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternally routing to the streaming parser via a [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ByteArrayInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintain boundary checks:**  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enforce `size >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, `total + size <= MAX_LENGTH`, and optionally per‐segment [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`size <= MAX_LENGTH`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the `PFB_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_LENGTH` minimum check *only* to verify the file is not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrivially short before streaming begins.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserve existing functionality:**  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The order and content of `pfbdata` remain identical—only the implementation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASCII segments continue to get “clear‐to‐mark” processing.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any callers of `[0m[1;35mgetPfbData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or downstream code find the same `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpfbdata`.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Rationale and benefits:**  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Peak memory** is now at most ~[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m× the final `pfbdata` length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone buffer in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ByteArrayOutputStream`, plus the transient `buf` of [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No per‐segment `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` lists or duplicate buffers.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The cumulative size check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MAX_LENGTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains intact, preventing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madversarial PFBs larger than the heuristic cap.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Streaming is compatible with existing fuzzer harnesses—no fuzz logic modified.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Mitigations and side‐effects:**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ByteArrayOutputStream grows its internal buffer; by pre‐allocating with [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_LENGTH`, we avoid doubling overhead.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream truly needs random access to `pfbdata`, it still gets a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontiguous `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code gains slight CPU overhead from chunked reads, which is acceptable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompared to preventing OOME.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. **No external or harness changes:**  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All modifications are contained within `PfbParser.java`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPDFBox callers, Jazzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unchanged.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests that expect the same `pfbdata` content will continue to pass.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Initial issue: A Java fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJazzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m crash due to `OutOfMemoryError` when [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforcing a `MAX_LENGTH` limit, replacing in-memory byte-array accumulation with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincremental I/O and segment-by-segment processing.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Patch result: Compilation errors in `PfbParser.java`—the symbols [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CARRIAGE_RETURN` and `LINE_FEED` are undefined, causing build failure in the [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exception thrown:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Context: The fuzzer calls `[0m[1;35mPDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich ultimately invokes `PfbParser.parsePfb` via PDFBox’s font-loading code paths.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Key observations:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The original implementation reads the entire InputStream into a single [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35min.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • All segments are stored in memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `List<byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m>`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before reassembling [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Changed constructors:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` now wraps the stream in a [0m                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` now wraps the byte array in a [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ByteArrayInputStream` and calls `parsePfbStream`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduced `[0m[1;35mparsePfbStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Reads and validates a fixed-size header [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PFB_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_LENGTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mark`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`reset`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Iterates segments: reads a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte little-endian size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`readUint32LE`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Uses `copyFully` for binary segments, `clearToMarkStream` for ASCII segments[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Aggregates output into a `ByteArrayOutputStream` of capped capacity.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Sets `this.pfbdata` and populates `this.lengths` accordingly [0m[1;39m([0m[33mascii[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation errors stem from two undefined constants, `CARRIAGE_RETURN` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LINE_FEED`, referenced in the newly added `clearToMarkStream` helper. To resolve [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis, we must declare these constants in `PfbParser.java`, matching the pattern of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother PFB markers. No other parts of the code require adjustment.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Steps to Implement the Patch  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Reapply the streaming-parser changes from the last patch attempt in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PfbParser.java`, ensuring methods `parsePfbStream`, `readUint32LE`, `copyFully`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `clearToMarkStream` are present.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the class-level constants section [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust after `EOF_MARKER`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add two new [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`private static final int` constants:  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * Carriage return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCR[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m byte value.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int CARRIAGE_RETURN = [0m[1;36m0x0D[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * Line feed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m byte value.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int LINE_FEED = [0m[1;36m0x0A[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Verify that no other undefined symbols remain.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Rebuild the FontBox module; ensure the compilation error is gone.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Consistency: Other PFB markers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`START_MARKER`, `ASCII_MARKER`, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BINARY_MARKER`, `EOF_MARKER`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are declared as `int`; CR and LF should use the same[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Preservation of functionality: The new CR/LF constants enable [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`clearToMarkStream` to strip carriage returns and line feeds from ASCII segments as[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended, preserving the behavior of removing DOS/UNIX line endings in PFB ASCII [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparts.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Minimal impact: No external libraries, harness code, or tests are modified. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExisting logic, including the enforcement of `MAX_LENGTH` and streaming behavior, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains intact.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Byte vs. int comparison: In `clearToMarkStream`, a `byte b` is compared [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magainst these `int` constants. Java widens `b` to an int automatically, so the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparison remains correct. No further adjustments needed.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Upstream/downstream integration: Since only constants are added, the semantics[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof reading and filtering segments are unchanged. Downstream consumers [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`PDType1Font`, `PDFTextStripper`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will see the same PFB data layout.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Compile `fontbox` module to completion.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Run existing unit and integration tests for PfbParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Execute fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify the OutOfMemory [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigations are in place and no regressions occur.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis targeted addition restores correct compilation and honors the intended [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstreaming-parser design without altering external or harness code.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
